            "post": {
                "tags": [
                    "Authentication"
                ],
                "summary": "Second step for OAuth Mechanism",

                "consumes": [

                "produces": [

                        "type": "string"

                    {
                        "name": "grant_type",
                        "in": "formData",
                        "description": "OAuth grant_type - must be one of the following: 'authorization_code', 'refresh_token'",

                        "type": "string"

                        "name": "redirect_uri",

                    {
                        "name": "code",

                        "type": "string"

                        "name": "refresh_token",
